9-0 Decks at Grand Prix Barcelona 2016
======================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on April 16, 2016 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20170709072651im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Frank Karsten and Tobi Henke











After nine grueling rounds of *Shadows over Innistrad* Sealed Deck, seven players took their spot at the top of the standings with pristine records of 9-0 still intact: Platinum pros Marcio Carvalho and William Jensen (pictured below), GP champions Damien Bouillot and Brian Braun-Duin, as well as Geoffrey Martinelle, Ferran Vila, and Francisco Rubio.


![](https://media.wizards.com/2016/events/gpbar16/BCN16_9-0s.jpg)


Check out the lists of their decks and pools here. You can load them up on Magic Online too if you want to try building your own decks from this source material!







#### Marcio Carvalho, 9-0 at Grand Prix Barcelona 2016


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
